		success: function(data) {
			$(document).trigger('loginStatus', [data]);
			$(document).trigger('adminview',[data]);
		},
		error: function(xhr, textStatus){
			var data = { logged_in:null, error:textStatus };
			$(document).trigger('loginStatus', [data]);
		}
	});

	$('.commentsheading &gt; span &gt; a').click(function(){

	});
	}
});


$(document).ready(function(){
	$.ajax({
		url: "http://reason.com/ajax/commenthandle",
		dataType: 'json',
		success: function(data) {
			$(document).trigger('loginStatus', [data]);
			$(document).trigger('adminview',[data]);
		},
		error: function(xhr, textStatus){
			var data = { logged_in:null, error:textStatus };
			$(document).trigger('loginStatus', [data]);
		}
	});

	$('.commentsheading &gt; span &gt; a').click(function(){
		document.location.hash = 'comment';
	});

	if (window.location.hash.match(/^#comment/)) {
			var cctrl = $('.commentcontrol'), cctnr = $('#commentcontainer');
			cctrl.addClass('open');
			cctnr.show();
			$('#commentform.cancomment').show();
		
	}else{
			var cctrl = $('.commentcontrol'), cctnr = $('#commentcontainer');
			cctnr.hide();
			cctrl.removeClass('open');
			cctrl.one('click', function(e) {
				cctrl.addClass('open');
				cctnr.show();
				$('#commentform.cancomment').show();
			});
	}
	if($.cookie('fontSize')) {
		var fontSize = $.cookie('fontSize');
 		$('article.post').css({'font-size':fontSize});
 		$('ul.posts').css({'font-size':fontSize});
 	}

	// SIDR PANELS

	$('#mobile-nav-toggle').unbind('onclick');
	$('#mobile-nav-toggle').sidr({
		displace: false,
		name: 'sidr-main',
		source: '#site-navigation',
		side:'right'
	});
	jQuery('#sidr-main .sidr-class-closemenu a').click(function(){
		jQuery.sidr('close', 'sidr-main');
		jQuery('.small-share').show();
	});
	jQuery('.container_24').click(function(){
		jQuery.sidr('close', 'sidr-main');
	});
	jQuery('#mobile-nav-toggle').click(function(){
		jQuery('.small-share').hide();
	});


	$('#mobile-trending-toggle').unbind('onclick');
	jQuery('#mobile-trending-toggle').sidr({
		displace: false,
		name: 'sidr-trending',
		source: '#trending-navigation',
		side: 'left'
	});
	jQuery('#sidr-trending .sidr-class-closemenu a').click(function(){

        jQuery('.small-share').show();
	});
	jQuery('.container_24').click(function(){
		jQuery.sidr('close', 'sidr-trending');
	});
	jQuery('#mobile-trending-toggle').click(function(){
		jQuery('.small-share').hide();
	});
	jQuery(window).resize(function () {
		if (jQuery(window).width() &gt; 700) {
			jQuery.sidr('close', 'sidr-main');
			jQuery.sidr('close', 'sidr-trending');
		}
	});

	// let's do this in jquery so we're sure it's stacked
	$('textarea').focus( function() {
		jQuery.sidr('close', 'sidr-main');
		jQuery.sidr('close', 'sidr-trending');
	});
	// $.sidr('open', 'sidr-main');

	function setScaleable(x) {
		originalval = $('head meta[name=viewport]').attr('content');
		newval = originalval.replace(/(user-scalable=)\d{1,9}/g, '$1'+x);
		if (originalval.localeCompare(newval)) {
			$('head meta[name=viewport]').attr('content', newval);
		} else {
			$('head meta[name=viewport]').attr('content', originalval+', user-scalable='+x);
		}
	}

	//we don't want the screen to scale up when we select a text item, so we're going to prevent it by turning it on and off as we enter and leave
	$('textarea, input').on('focusin', function() {
		setScaleable(0);
	});

	$('textaream, input').on('focusout', function() {
		setScaleable(1);
	});

	// there's some visual element eh when people leave the screen, possibly because of fixed position
	// and element destruction order. We're going to simply hide these items on the way out to make sure
	// they don't jump around
	$( window ).unload(function() {
  		$('#nav1').hide();
  		$('#sidr-main').hide();
  		$('#sidr-trending').hide();
	});


	$("a#sidr-id-fontbigger").click(function() {
 		$('ul.posts').css('font-size', function(index,value) {
 			var fontSize = parseInt(value) + 1 + 'px';
	 		$.cookie('fontSize',fontSize, { path: '/', expires: 7 });
	 		return fontSize;
 		});
 		$('#right-col').css('font-size', function(index,value) {

  		$('article.post').css('font-size', function(index,value) {
 			var fontSize = parseInt(value) + 1 + 'px';
	 		$.cookie('fontSize',fontSize, { path: '/', expires: 7 });
	 		return fontSize;
 		});
	});

	$("a#sidr-id-fontsmaller").click(function() {
 		$('ul.posts').css('font-size', function(index,value) {
 			var fontSize = parseInt(value) - 1 + 'px';
	 		$.cookie('fontSize',fontSize, { path: '/', expires: 7 });

window.USERSTATE = {logged_in:null};
$(document).bind('loginStatus', function(e, d) {
	$.extend(window.USERSTATE, d);
});

	$(document).bind('adminview', function(e, d) {
		if(d.isadmin){
			$("body").addClass("adminlogin");
			window.ADMININFO = JSONObject= {
				"baseurl":"http://reason.com/",
				"showeditbutton":1,
				"showadminbar":1,
				"showcommentcontrols":1,
				"usersettingsurl":"http://reason.com/admin/users//modify",
				"commentactions" : 0};
			$.getScript("/media/js/navtools.js");
		}
	});

function updateCountdowns() {
	editbuttons = $('button.comment_edit:visible');
	if (editbuttons.length) {
		editbuttons.each(function() {
			timeremaining = $(this).data('editwindow-remaining');
			if (--timeremaining &lt; 0) {
				$(this).text('edit timer expired');
				$(this).fadeOut(); //no need for further time update; we only poll visibles
			} else {
				$(this).text('edit ('+timeremaining+' seconds remaining)');
				$(this).data('editwindow-remaining', timeremaining);
			}
		})
	} else {
		//no reason to keep this running when there's nothing to update
		clearInterval(countdownTimer);
	}
}

var countdownTimer = null;

$(document).bind('loginStatus', function(e,d){
	servertime = Number(d.unixtime);
	editing_window_seconds = Number(d.editing_window_seconds);
	if (d.logged_in) {
		userID = d.user_id;
		var handle = $("#user_login_control")
		.html('&lt;p&gt;You are currently logged in as: &lt;strong&gt;&lt;a href="http://reason.com/users/manage" class="handle"&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;. &lt;a href="http://reason.com/users/logout"&gt;&lt;span&gt;Sign Out&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt;')
		.find('.handle')
		handle.text(d.handle)
		handle.attr('href', handle.attr('href')+'/'+userID);
		//look for all the editable comments by this user
		$('div#commentcontainer li[data-user-id='+userID+']').each(function( index ) {
			commenttimestamp = Number($(this).data('comment-timestamp'));
			elapsedtime = servertime - commenttimestamp;
			if (elapsedtime &lt; editing_window_seconds) {
				secondsremaining = editing_window_seconds - elapsedtime;
				$(this).find('button.comment_edit').show().data('editwindow-remaining', secondsremaining);
			}
		});
		countdownTimer = setInterval(updateCountdowns, 1E3);
	} else {
		$("#user_login_control").html('&lt;a href="http://reason.com/users/login"&gt;&lt;span&gt;Login&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/a&gt; or &lt;a href="http://reason.com/users/register"&gt;&lt;span&gt;Sign-up&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/a&gt;');
	}
});

(function(){
	var threadedCommentRepliesActive=null;
	var cb = $('#commentcontainer');

	function cmtLoginStatusHandler(e,d) {
		var lc = $('#commentform'), clr = $('.comment_login_require');
		if (d.logged_in) {
			clr.hide();
			lc.addClass('cancomment');
			lc.find('.logged_in_as').remove();
			var handle = lc.children('form')
			.prepend('&lt;div class="logged_in_as"&gt;&lt;p&gt;You are currently logged in as &lt;a href="http://reason.com/users/manage/'+d.user_id+'" class="handle"&gt;&lt;/a&gt;. Not you? &lt;a href="http://reason.com/users/logout"&gt;Sign out&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;')
			.find('.handle');
			handle.text(d.handle);
			handle.attr('a', handle.attr('a')+'/'+d.user_id);
			lc.show();
			threadedCommentReplies(true);
			editComments(true);
		} else if (d.logged_in===false) {
			clr.show();
			lc.removeClass('cancomment');
			threadedCommentReplies(false);
		} else {
			clr.html('&lt;p&gt;Oops, something went wrong and we can\'t tell if you\'re logged in. Please referesh and try again.&lt;/p&gt;');
		}
	}

	function threadedCommentReplies(activate){
		var cb = $('#commentcontainer');
		if (activate) {
			cb.find('.comment_reply').show();
			cb.find('.comment_reply_msg').hide();
			if (!threadedCommentRepliesActive &amp;&amp; (typeof(CommentReplyForm) !== "undefined")) {
				var template = CommentReplyForm.preparetemplate('commentform');
				var crf = new CommentReplyForm(template);
				crf.bindHandlers('li.com-block button.comment_reply');
				var previewurl = $('#commentform form').attr('action').replace(/\/post$/, '/preview');
				CommentPreview.bindHandlers(template, template.find(':button.preview'), previewurl);
				CommentPreview.bindHandlers($('#commentform'), $('#commentform :button.preview'), previewurl);
			}
		} else {
			cb.find('.comment_reply').hide();
			cb.find('.comment_reply_msg').show();
			cb.find('.leave-comment').hide();
		}
	}

	function editComments(activate) {
		var cb = $('#commentcontainer');
		if (activate) {
			//we find only the ones made visible during initialization; no reason to bind the rest.
			// active_edit_buttons = $('button.comment_edit:visible');
			if (typeof(CommentEditForm) !== "undefined") {
				var template = CommentEditForm.preparetemplate('commenteditform');
				var crf = new CommentEditForm(template);
				crf.bindHandlers('button.comment_edit:visible');
			}
		} else {
			cb.find('button.comment_edit').hide();
		}
	}
	$(document).bind('loginStatus', cmtLoginStatusHandler);


})();

        <a href="http://reason.com/blog">

      <article class="post">
       <header class="mainheading">
        <h2 class="title">
         <a href="http://reason.com/blog/2012/12/28/boy-not-making-bombs-arrested-for-having">
          Boy, Not Making Bombs, Arrested for Having Things Cops Think Could Blow Up (And For Drawings That Spooked a Teacher)
         </a>
         <span class="editor" pid="177411">
         </span>
        </h2>
        <p class="byline">
         <a href="http://reason.com/people/brian-doherty/all" rel="author">
          Brian Doherty
         </a>
         <span class="pipe">
          |
         </span>
         <time datetime="2012-12-28T22:51:00+00:00">
          Dec. 28, 2012 5:51 pm
         </time>
        </p>
        <aside class="social clearfix">
         <div data-naytev-link="http://reason.com/blog/2012/12/28/boy-not-making-bombs-arrested-for-having" data-naytev-share-horizontal="" data-naytev-tweet="Boy, Not Making Bombs, Arrested for Having Things Cops Think Could Blow Up (And For Drawings That Spooked a Teacher)" data-naytev-with-share-counts="">
         </div>
         <div id="leftover_sharing">
          <ul>
           <li class="reddit share_item">
            <a href="http://www.reddit.com/submit" onclick="var newLoc = 'http://www.reddit.com/submit?url='+encodeURIComponent('http://reason.com/blog/2012/12/28/boy-not-making-bombs-arrested-for-having'); window.open(newLoc, 'submit');return false;">
            </a>
           </li>
           <li id="spritz">
            <a class="spritzbutton" href="#" id="clicktospritz_177411" onclick="return false;">
             Spritz
            </a>
            <div id="spritzer_177411" style="display:none;">
            </div>
            <script>
             var SpritzSettings = {
									clientId: "eb6c148c66f0e0a73",
									redirectUri: "http://reason.com/login_success.html"
								};

								    var spritzController = null;
									function spritz_177411() {
										function spritz_177411_visibility() {
											$('#spritzer_177411').toggle();

										function spritz_177411init() {
										    var onSpritzifySuccess = function(spritzText) {

       </header>
       <div class="p402_premium">
        <div class="entry postcontent">
         <p>
          The Comic Book Legal Defense Fund is
          <a href="http://cbldf.org/2012/12/doodles-lead-to-new-jersey-students-arrest/">
           publicizing an interesting little story
          </a>
          out of Galloway
Township in New Jersey:
         </p>
         <p>
         </p>
         <blockquote>
          <p>
           When a 16-year-old New Jersey boy doodled in his notebook on
Tuesday, December 18, he probably didnt expect to be arrested by
the end of the day. However, when school officials saw the
sketches, which they state appeared to be of weapons, and the boy

           <a href="http://www.pressofatlanticcity.com/communities/hammonton_egg-harbor-city/cedar-creek-student-had-chemicals-at-home-that-could-be/article_e129dbde-498a-11e2-ad39-0019bb2963f4.html">
            demonstrated
behavior that caused them to be concerned
           </a>
           , the police were
called.
          </p>
          <p>
           A subsequent search of the boys home led to his arrest because
they found several electronic parts and chemicals. He was charged
with the possession of an explosive device and put in juvenile
detention.
          </p>
          <p>
           The details on what was precisely in the drawings are sketchy,
as are the details on the behavior that caused concern. The school
claims the drawings were of weapons, but the boys mother told
various press outlets that, 
           <a href="http://www.myfoxphilly.com/story/20385390/fi">
            He drew a glove with
flames coming out of it
           </a>
           . If true, then the drawing wouldnt be
out of place in the notebook of any teenager who loves comic
books.
          </p>
          <p>
           At no point in time did the boy threaten the school, school
officials, or his classmates. He cooperated fully with authorities,
and a search of the school itself found nothing dangerous....
          </p>
         </blockquote>
         <p>
          Lest you think it is inherently suspicious a young man would
have chemicals or electronic parts, note that his school is,
according to a
          <a href="http://www.pressofatlanticcity.com/communities/hammonton_egg-harbor-city/cedar-creek-student-had-chemicals-at-home-that-could-be/article_e129dbde-498a-11e2-ad39-0019bb2963f4.html">
           Press
of Atlantic City account
          </a>
          , "a magnet school with programs
focusing on engineering and environmental sciences and specializing
in hands-on learning." And his mom
          <a href="http://www.myfoxphilly.com/story/20385390/fi">
           told
MyFoxPhilly.com
          </a>
          that her son had a "passion for collecting old
stuff, taking it apart and rebuilding things."
         </p>
         <p>
          Also of interest from that story, a school superintendent says
he's:
         </p>
         <blockquote>
          <p>
           "thankful that we had a staff member that (saw something
that) caused her some concern, and that she had the sense to report
it to school officials. These are things that teachers receive
training on all the time."
          </p>
         </blockquote>
         <div class="ym" id="ym_1044036704457308825">
         </div>
         <script type="text/javascript">
          (function(e,t){if(t._ym===void 0){t._ym="";var m=e.createElement("script");m.type="text/javascript",m.async=!0,m.src="//static.yieldmo.com/ym.m5.js",(e.getElementsByTagName("head")[0]||e.getElementsByTagName("body")[0]).appendChild(m)}else t._ym instanceof String||void 0===t._ym.chkPls||t._ym.chkPls()})(document,window);
         </script>
         <p>
          Most interesting detail from that Press of Atlantic City
story:
         </p>
         <blockquote>
          <p>
           Police Chief Pat Moran stressed Tuesday night no threats were
made by the student and there was no indication there was any
danger posed to anyone or property at the school.
          </p>
          <p>
           There was no indication he was making a bomb, or using a bomb
or detonating a bomb, he said.
          </p>
         </blockquote>
         <p>
          Sounds like a good collar to me, boys!
         </p>
        </div>

	else document.write(unescape(l[i]));}
	//]]&gt;
             </script>
            </strong>

           <!--Comment Body-->
           <div class="content">
            <p>
             When I was a kid, we had illegal fireworks(at least they would
be illegal today), I think they were just little sticks of dynamite
that would blow a 5 gallon metal bucket 100 ft into the air and
shred it to shrapnel.
            </p>
            <p>
             We would tie a rock to them and throw them into the water to
watch the huge explosion of water that would result.
            </p>
            <p>
             We blew up practically everything we could get our hands on that
we wouldn't get beaten by our parents for blowing up.
            </p>
            <p>
             One time we blew up a can of gasoline and the flaming
projectiles from it caught my uncles barn on fire. Luckily we were
able to put it out before it did much damage, but that was close.
Can't even remember the times that I came close to blowing off
fingers or getting injured by flying debris. Good times they
were.
            </p>
           </div>

          <li class="com-block reply5" data-comment-id="comment_3458222" data-comment-timestamp="1356753184" data-user-id="143" id="comment_3458222">
           <p class="meta">
            <strong>
             <a href="http://madlibertarianguy.net" rel="nofollow">
              mad libertarian guy
             </a>
            </strong>
            <span class="pipe">
             |
            </span>
            <strong>
             <time datetime="2012-12-29T04:53:04+00:00">
              12.28.12 @ 11:53PM
             </time>
            </strong>
            <span class="pipe">
             |
            </span>
            <a class="permalink" href="#comment_3458222">
             #
            </a>
           </p>
           <!--Comment Body-->
           <div class="content">
            <blockquote>
             Prior to 1995 there was no mention of coyotes in
Maryland statute or regulation and it was unclear what, if any,
management options were permissible for this species. Realizing
these inconsistencies, DNR supported legislation that provided for
the legal classification of coyotes as a "Fur-Bearing Mammal",
subject to several sunset clauses. This authorized the Department
of Natural Resources (DNR) to independently develop management
strategies and harvest regulations for this species. Subsequent
amendments prescribed certain management options to be instituted
by DNR.
             <br/>
             <br/>
             Specifically these amendments allow for the incidental take of
coyotes while a hunter is legally pursuing other game species, and
a year round harvest season by predator calling. The amendments
further authorized DNR to establish a trapping season for coyotes
with harvest regulations determined by DNR. Trapping seasons are
established annually by regulation and are concurrent with fox
trapping seasons in individual counties.
             <br/>
             <br/>
             During the 2000 legislative session the General Assembly repealed
the sunset clause provisions, thus affording the coyote permanent
statutory classification as a "Fur-Bearing Mammal".
            </blockquote>
            <p>
             Hunt away, my friend. Look in your state's annual hunting guide
for seasons, if there are any. I've yet to see a state in which the
coyote isn't an open season game animal.
            </p>
           </div>

           <!--Comment Body-->
           <div class="content">
            <p>
             We loved to put aerosol cans by the dozens inside a barrel with
a lot of tender and set on fire to watch it explode. One barrel
even got seriously air borne.
            </p>
            <p>
             There was an industrial dump several miles from the neighborhood
that we would trek too and bring back supplies to an abandoned
tobacco barn we renovated as a club house. We built a hang glider
out of sheets of plastic and other supplies and jumped off the roof
of the building. Almost got killed, but the fun I had as a kid was
off the charts Tom Sawyer.
            </p>
           </div>

           <!--Comment Body-->
           <div class="content">
            <p>
             I saw a PSA on blasting caps when I was 4 and immediately hopped
on my tricycle and went looking for blasting caps. I didn't find
any but a few years later I found out my brother was setting them
off with a dry cell battery(just like in the PSA!). By the time I
reached the IED-experimenting age I had to use Estes rocket motor
igniters in my own projects because they started carefully
accounting for blasting caps and you couldn't easily find them just
lying around anymore.
            </p>
           </div>

            <a class="permalink" href="#comment_3458147">
             #
            </a>
           </p>
           <!--Comment Body-->
           <div class="content">
            <p>
             I got a basic education in explosives from a 1950s "Book of
Knowledge" encyclopedia. The local public library branch filled in
much of the rest. The USDA and US Army also published excellent
information that was readily available for free to pocket change
from the county extension agent or Army surplus store. Old magic
books used to have detailed recipes for contact explosives and
flash powder. I still have all my fingers, eyesight and hearing
too. If the DHS/BATFE is reading I haven't practiced the "hobby" in
almost 35 years.
            </p>
           </div>

           <!--Comment Body-->
           <div class="content">
            <p>
             I can't believe nobody else made tennis ball grenades. My cousin
and I would poke a hole in a tennis ball and fill it with black
powder. Then we would plug the hole with a firecracker (usually a
black cat, but an M80 was better when we could get one).
            </p>
            <p>
             It's kind of odd, because now I have a great aversion to setting
off fireworks. Seeing the aftermath of do-it-yourself 4th of July
displays in the hospital has shifted my opinion of the
entertainment value of explosives.
            </p>
           </div>

             trump card before I head out for the
day...
            </p>
            <p>
             NICKLEBACK!!!!
            </p>

             **Lays open cards on table. Folds arms.**
            </p>

           <div class="content">
            <p>
             It's not too much to ask. Medical expatriation. I am practicing
medicine for a private hospital outfit, and they needed an
extremely qualified surgeon. I happen to be one (FACS). Bonus
points were awarded for language skills. Extra bonus points were
awarded for an extended contractual stay. Doubleplus bonus points
awarded for experience with rural medicine and complicated cases.
Needless to say, they bent over backwards to meet my requests,
including shielding me from FATCA as much as the law allows
(possibly then some). Under UKR medical law, my malpractice
insurance is peanuts compared to what I was paying in the states
(110k USD/year).
            </p>
            <p>
             Without going too much more into it, it's more beneficial for
me, overall, to have fled the USA and ObamneyCare.
            </p>
            <p>
             Yeah, -1C is ~31F. It was
             <em>
              much
             </em>
             colder earlier this
month ~(-32C), and it's very windy in Donets'k and the surrounding
area oblast'. Normally this time of year, it's around 20-25F, so we
have a bit of a warm spell.
            </p>
            <p>
             I also hope to maybe find the future Mrs. Groovus here, if Fate
permits.
            </p>
           </div>

      <script>
       $(document).ready(function() {
    	//no point in binding to swipe events if there's no touch support in the browser (and it goofs up selection)
		if ('ontouchstart' in window) {
			//in an effort to reduce false horizontal swipes from bold vertical flicks on larger screens...
			swipeThreshold = 200;
			$("#content-col").swipe( {
				threshold: swipeThreshold,
				allowPageScroll: 'vertical',
			    swipeLeft:function(event, direction, distance, duration, fingerCount) {
			    	//we're going to put in a non-zero fingercount check here to exclude mouse drags
					if (fingerCount &amp;&amp; $('#nextpage').length &amp;&amp; $('#nextpage').attr("href").length) {
					    window.location.href=  $('#nextpage').attr("href");
					}
			    },
			    swipeRight:function(event, direction, distance, duration, fingerCount) {
			    	//we're going to put in a non-zero fingercount check here to exclude mouse drags
					if (fingerCount &amp;&amp; $('#previouspage').length &amp;&amp; $('#previouspage').attr("href").length) {
				    	window.location.href = $('#previouspage').attr("href");
					}
			    }
			});
		}
    });
      </script>

        <script>
         $(function(){
	$("#topstoriessidebar .selector a").click(function(e){
		var $this=$(this), catref = $this.attr("data-category"),
			$sidebar = $this.parent().parent().parent();
		e.preventDefault();
		$sidebar.find('&gt; .selector &gt; li').removeClass('active');
		$this.parent().addClass('active');
		$sidebar.find('&gt; .inner &gt; .stories').hide().filter('[data-category='+catref+']').show();
	});
});
